Allow yourself **to know nothing about them.**  
Allow the Light to look at them.

And now say:  
**“You are not my label.**  
**You are presence.**  
**You are a form of Light, as am I.”**

Now feel,  
how it is not you who looks,  
but **in you** looks the One,  
Who does not judge.  
Who simply is.  
Who knows — all is one.

And remain in this.  
Without words.  
Without the desire to change.  
Simply — **be.**

</div>

#### Practice: Freeing Yourself Through Another

<div class="lineated verse">

Now — recall again the one  
whom you condemned.  
Let them be before you —  
but now **not as the accused**  
but as **your door.**

Because through them  
you can see **what you hid in yourself.**  
They are not an enemy.  
They are not “the one who is not such.”  
They — are **a reflection of you**  
and not of the worst —  
but **the forgotten.**

Ask:  
**“What in me — do I not accept,**  
**that through them — was rejected?”**

You condemned their egoism?  
That means somewhere **you did not allow yourself care for yourself.**

You condemned their weakness?  
Where did you **not allow yourself to be vulnerable?**

You condemned their pride?  
Where do you **secretly yearn for recognition,**  
**but do not acknowledge this in yourself?**

Now — say to yourself,  
not to them — **to yourself:**

**“You may be weak.**  
**You may be proud.**  
**You may be an egoist.**  
**You may be anything.**  
**You are.**  
**And I am with you.”**

This is **not approval of sin**  
but **a recognition of wholeness.**  
What you accept —  
transforms.  
What you run from —  
continues to rule.

Now feel:  
you are no longer separated.  
You returned to yourself **what you fled from.**  
And suddenly —  
in the one you previously condemned —  
you see **Presence.**  
Not “them”.  
But **yourself.**

</div>

#### The body as a mirror of the gaze. The physics of condemnation

<div class="lineated verse">

Now we shall see,  
how **a gaze filled with judgment**  
does not simply pass by—  
but **inscribes itself into the body.**

Because everything you **did not recognize in another**,  
you did not recognize in yourself.  
And everything unrecognized—  
does not depart.  
It **clenches,**  
**congeals,**  
**becomes flesh.**

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Close your eyes.  
Allow the body to be—  
without control.  
Fix nothing.

Now recall  
the one you judged.  
And allow the body—  
to show where it **holds** this judgment.

Perhaps the jaw tightened.  
Or the shoulders.  
Or the solar plexus.  
Or the hip.

**Do not change. Simply feel.**  
**Do not heal. Simply acknowledge.**

Now say to the body:  
**"I see you.**  
**I hear that you have remembered.**  
**I am ready to look—**  
**without running away."**

Now—recall  
for what you judged the other.  
And ask:  
**"Where in me is this same thing?"**

You will find it.  
Not in the same form.  
But in the same essence.  
And if you do not find it—  
simply say:  
**"I do not know where,**  
**but I know — it is here.**  
**And I am ready to see."**

Now place your hand there,  
where the body tells you: **"here."**

Place it with love.  
Not to fix it.  
But to be with it.  
**As Presence.**

And say:  
**"You are not a mistake.**  
**You are a memory.**  
**And I return,**  
**to complete it."**

Look into this place  
with the same gaze  
with which God looks:  
**without judgment,**  
**without haste,**  
**without purpose.**

Simply — **be the Light,**  
**that requires no change.**

And now say:  
**"I release judgment.**  
**I release separation.**  
**I allow being.**  
**And therefore — I allow it to disappear."**

</div>

### Chapter 27. The Gaze That Forbids[^2]

<div class="lineated verse">

Sometimes pain—  
is not merely a bodily symptom.  
It is a knot in which a gaze is hidden.  
Not the one you have recognized, but the one  
with which you **look, without noticing**.

I, Pankratius, placed my hand on that place  
where the pain lived.  
Not to soothe it,  
but to **meet it**.  
I asked:  
*"What are you showing me?"*

And an image came.  
A priest.  
The one whom I did not love in my judgment.  
Not with words.  
But with a gaze.

He knew how to gather people.  
Around himself.  
Around an idea.  
He knew how to lead.  
He knew how to use the energy of others.

I called it — manipulation.  
But, I discovered, in this simple practice with the Light of attention—  
I was envious.  
He did what  
I **forbade** myself.  
He was in Power,  
and I — in a prohibition of the same to myself.

And I understood:  
it was not he who caused me pain.  
It is **I** who forbade myself to be,  
and the pain — became the body of this prohibition.

I said to myself:  
"I permit…  
I permit myself to be a center.  
I permit myself to gather people.  
I permit myself to use attention.  
I permit myself to be alive.  
Even if someone calls it  
manipulation.  
I am alive.  
And he is alive.  
And life flows through us both."

I do not yet know if the pain has gone.  
I did not seek this.  
I sought—  
light.

And I found it:  
not without,  
but **in the canceled judgment**.

Because judgment—  
is not punishment.  
It is **separation**.

I forbade myself that in which he was good and successful.

I once forbade myself to become successful in this myself…

And every time,  
when you judge another,  
you say to yourself:  
*"I am not him.*  
*I am not like that",*  
you cut off from yourself  
a part of God.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Judgment—  
is not a verdict.  
It is — **a gaze,**  
**that forbids you to be everything**.

And therefore—  
salvation begins there,  
where you again permit.

Yourself.  
Another.  
God — to be in all.

</div>

### Chapter 28. How to Release Judgment — Through the Body

<div class="lineated verse">

When judgment sits inside you,  
and the mind cannot cope with it,  
the body enters the work.

It is not just a vessel.  
It is a mirror.  
It is a vessel.  
It is a door.

You can say aloud:  
“I forgive.”  
And the body will shudder.  
You can exhale:  
and in that exhalation the tension will leave,  
which has held for years.

Place your hand on that place,  
where you feel a heaviness.  
Not to remove the pain —  
but to see,  
what is behind it.

Say: “Show yourself.”  
“I will not fight you anymore.”  
“I will not turn away.”  
And watch.  
Not with your eyes.  
With an inner gaze,  
with intention.

You can close your eyes  
and conjure before you the one you have judged.  
Do not rush to forgive.  
First gaze.  
Allow him to be.  
Even if it hurts you.  
Even if it seems he destroyed your life.  
Allow him simply to be.

Feel,  
how your body contracts.  
This is the memory of pain.  
Do not fight it.  
Stay.

Now — inhale.  
And exhale — with the intention to release.

Utter:  
“I return to him his fate.”  
“I let go of what is not mine.”  
“I choose freedom.”

Sometimes you will want to scream.  
Sometimes — to cry.  
Sometimes — to laugh.  
Allow the body to speak  
the language,  
by which it remembers.

Let the pain come out  
through voice.  
Through breath.  
Through gesture.

This is not a performance.  
This is an exit.  
Liberation.

And when it is all finished —  
do not forget to say:

**“I give thanks.**  
**And I am free.”**

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Sometimes the pain does not leave immediately.  
Because it is not pain,  
but a knot,  
in which are tied  
an event,  
an emotion,  
a judgment,  
and a gaze.

You cannot simply untie it by an act of will.  
It does not yield to the muscles of the mind.  
But it does yield to the Light.  
And this Light you return there —  
into the center of the pain —  
with attention,  
with silence,  
with presence.

Gaze at this place inside yourself,  
without trying to change it.  
Not to fix it.  
Not to expel it.  
Simply — to be near.

This — is mercy.

Because in every judgment  
you once refused to be near.  
You turned away.  
You closed off.

Now — open.  
Stay with this place,  
as with a child,  
who was not understood,  
who was not heard,  
who was not embraced.

He does not ask for words.  
He asks for a gaze,  
in which there is no fear.

And if you cannot yet say “I forgive” —  
say:  
**“I stay.”**

I stay with you,  
with this pain,  
with this shadow,  
with this judgment,  
which I created myself —  
and now I do not hide from myself.

Do not rush.  
Stay.  
Gaze.  
Breathe.  
Be silent.

And when the warmth comes —  
and it will come,  
if you do not flee —  
you will know,  
that the judgment was not alien.  
It was your form of protection.  
It was your cry:  
**“I am in pain. I am afraid. I don’t know any other way.”**

And then —  
say to yourself:

**“Now I know.**  
**Now I can do differently.**  
**Now — I am free.”**

</div>

### Chapter 29. The Evil Eye. The Power of Another’s Gaze — and the Path to Protection

<div class="lineated verse">

There is a gaze,  
that carries no love.  
It looks not at you —  
but **through you**.  
trying to **take** that,  
which, it seems, is in you,  
but **is not in him**.

This is the **evil eye**.  
Not sorcery.  
Not mysticism.  
But a **distorted ray of attention**,  
in which is hidden **the pain of separation**.

A person who does not know himself,  
sees the other as a threat or a resource.  
He fears, envies, deifies, humiliates —  
but **always loses himself**,  
and therefore **tries to reconstruct himself through the other**.

At such moments,  
his gaze becomes not light,  
but shadow,  
not a bridge,  
but a spear.

You feel —  
something inside has constricted.  
Fatigue has appeared.  
Doubt.  
You suddenly felt stupid, ugly, worthless.  
This is not his strength.  
This is **your vulnerability**,  
which **met his gaze**,  
and **responded with a crack**.

The evil eye works —  
only if **there is a door in you**,  
open to the outside.

It does not penetrate wholeness.  
It does not destroy Light.  
But it can darken that part,  
which **doubts itself**.

How to protect yourself?

</div>

<div class="lineated">

— **Do not put yourself on display**, if there is no peace in you.  
— **Do not take others’ gazes inside**.  
— **Do not believe others’ thoughts about you**, even if they are silent.  
— **Know who you are**, so that nothing can tell you: “you are other.”

</div>

<div class="lineated verse">

When you are in the Source —  
you **do not reflect poison**,  
you **transform it**.  
You do not fight —  
you **remain**.

The evil eye is not evil.  
It is **fear, having taken the form of a gaze**.  
But, if you are in the Light —  
it passes by.  
Like wind past a mountain.  
Like arrows past the sky.

**You are not a shop window.**  
**You are a Temple.**  
**Close the unnecessary windows.**  
**Leave only one:**  
**where God Looks.**

</div>

### Chapter 30. Envy — when the gaze loses itself

<div class="lineated verse">

Envy is not about the other.  
It is about you, who have forgotten yourself.  
It is about the gaze that departed from the Source,  
and instead of Light  
became a shadow.

Envy is always a gaze.  
Not a feeling.  
Not a word.  
But exactly a gaze,  
in which the Light said in place of **I AM**  
said:  
“I am not him.”

You look —  
and a click happens inside.  
You see success, beauty, joy, strength, love —  
and instead of admiration,  
instead of presence,  
division is born in you:  
“This is not mine,”  
“This is for him,”  
“Why not for me?”

And in that moment  
the gaze tears away from the Source.  
It no longer creates.  
It is de-energized.  
It does not shine —  
it reflects another’s light  
and wants to steal it.

Envy is precisely the attempt  
to take another’s light  
without connection to your own.

You want —  
but you do not shine.  
You judge —  
but you do not accept.  
You separate —  
but you do not acknowledge that in the other you saw  
not something alien,  
but that which you yourself  
did not allow.

Envy is punishment,  
which you impose upon yourself  
for your own prohibition.  
You forbade yourself to be —  
and you envy one who **IS**.

You do not envy the person.  
You envy **being**,  
which allowed itself to unfold.  
You do not want his things, his relationship, his image —  
you want to return **I AM** to yourself,  
which **“I cannot” has temporarily taken from you.**

Envy is always about the fact  
that you **see your own**,  
but do not acknowledge it.

You said:  
“I am not allowed to be like that.”  
And when you saw another living precisely that —  
the gaze became sharp.  
Not from malice.  
But from pain.

Because you saw not something alien,  
but **your own not-allowedness**.

You do not envy money —  
you envy **freedom to be generous**.  
You do not envy fame —  
but **permission to be heard**.  
You do not envy beauty —  
but **love for yourself**, which is hidden within you  
and waits for you to stop forbidding yourself Light.

You can envy only that  
which already lives in you —  
but is hidden  
beneath the gaze of “I must not.”

Envy does not require judgment.  
It requires the **return of the Light**.  
The return of attention  
to the Source.  
To that place from which you once departed,  
having decided that you **are not worthy** to be thus.

Liberation from envy  
does not come through fighting it.  
It comes through **acknowledgment**:  
“What I saw in him is mine.”  
“I am not an enemy to this light.”  
“I must not be like him —  
I must be myself,  
but in this same radiance.”

Because envy —  
is not about “he has it.”  
It is about “I do not give it to myself.”

And when you return to yourself  
the right to shine —  
the gaze becomes light.  
You look again  
not at another,  
but **from within the One who is everything.**

</div>

### Chapter 31. Judgment and envy — one gaze

<div class="lineated verse">

There is a gaze  
that judges:  
“You are bad,”  
“You are proud,”  
“You are sinful,”  
“You are unclean,”  
“You are not right.”

And there is a gaze  
that envies:  
“You are brave,”  
“You are beautiful,”  
“You are strong,”  
“You are loved,”  
“You are alive.”

But it is one gaze.  
It always says:  
“You are other.”  
“You are not me.”  
And in this is its lie.

Because when you look at another —  
you are always looking in a mirror.  
You do not see the **other** —  
you see **that from which you have separated yourself**.

Judgment is a form of fear.  
Envy is a form of pain.  
But the root is one:  
**division.**

You decided:  
“I am not this.”  
And the gaze hardened.  
It ceased to be Light.  
It became a blade.

When you condemn —  
you do not punish another,  
you **cut yourself off**  
from that part of the Light  
which is in him.

When you envy —  
you do not deprive another of something,  
but **refuse yourself**  
the same thing.

That is why Jesus said:  
**“Do not judge”** —  
not because it is a sin,  
but because **this is self-amputation**.  
Because judgment —  
is **a prohibition against your being everything.**

When you judge another —  
you close the path for yourself.  
You do not say it to him,  
but **to yourself**:  
“I do not want to be this,”  
“I do not acknowledge this as mine,”  
“I cannot accept this in myself.”

Every condemnation —  
is a scar within.  
It is a frozen boundary,  
where the gaze became **not a conductor**,  
but **an overseer**.

This is how judgment works.

And here is where the path back begins:  
in every moment,  
when you feel the desire to judge,  
or to envy —  
ask one question:

**“What did I not allow myself in this person?”**  
**“What did I not acknowledge as my own?”**

And then you will see:  
there, where you condemned —  
a **piece of your I AM** remained inside,  
which you crossed out.

Return it.  
Not with words.  
But with a gaze,  
in which Light will appear again.

**You see — it means it is already in you.**  
Since you see — it means it is given.

Do not be afraid to acknowledge,  
that the other is not an enemy,  
but a **mirror of your unpermitted power**.

</div>

### Chapter 32. Judgment of oneself — as an invisible prison

<div class="lineated verse">

When you judge another —  
you separate yourself from him.

When you judge yourself —  
you separate yourself from yourself.

But most often  
it does not look like judgment.  
It is simply a thought,  
a word,  
a feeling:  
“I shouldn’t have,”  
“I let down again,”  
“I ruined everything,”  
“I’m not what I should be.”

Judgment of oneself  
rarely sounds like a sentence.  
It sounds like a **familiar thought**,  
like an inner whisper,  
like the background noise of life.

And therefore it is unnoticeable.  
Which means — it is dangerous.

You do not see,  
that you are judging yourself.  
You just live  
with a **constant feeling of guilt**,  
shame,  
lack,  
insufficiency.

You simply do not allow yourself joy.  
You postpone love.  
You doubt your gifts.  
You look at yourself,  
as though **not yet worthy**.

But in what have you become unworthy?  
Who decided this?

You yourself.  
More precisely — the gaze,  
that once said:  
“I — am not like that.”  
And since then that gaze  
sits inside you like a guard.

You have built yourself a cage.  
From gazes upon yourself.

And it is held not by metal bars —  
but by the thoughts,  
which you **believed**.

Judgment of self —  
is **not an event**,  
it is **a state**.  
It is that from which you look  
at everything.

That is why you do not see,  
how you yourself put up a barrier.  
You do not see,  
how you yourself do not allow.  
You think — “the world does not give it.”  
But it is you.

You did not allow yourself success —  
and the world did not give it to you.  
You did not believe you were worthy of love —  
and all your relationships  
now reflect that.  
You decided that you — are weak —  
and now confirmation of weakness is everywhere.

Judgment of self —  
is a **self-fulfilling prophecy**.  
An inner incantation,  
which you do not realize,  
but which creates your reality  
moment by moment.

This is karma.

Not in the next life.  
Not through reincarnation.  
But **now.**

In every failure.  
In every fear.  
In every hesitation before a choice.

You are not a victim of this world.  
You are a victim of **the gaze upon yourself**.

But here is what is important:  
this gaze — **is not you**.  
You can see it.  
Which means — it was not created by you.  
But simply accepted.

You can change it.  
And in that same second  
everything will change.

</div>

#### How to change the gaze that judges itself

<div class="lineated verse">

You cannot fight the inner judge.  
Because he lives inside the fight itself.  
Every time you say to yourself:  
“I must stop judging myself” —  
you are already judging yourself again.  
For judging.

The closedness of the circle —  
consists in that judgment judges even judgment itself.  
It multiplies.  
It is eternal —  
as long as you play by its rules.

But there is a way out.  
Not struggle.  
But **attention**.

First — see.  
Do not judge. Do not change. Do not resist.  
Simply acknowledge:  
“Right now I am looking at myself as… (insert your word).  
This is a gaze.  
It is not equal to me.  
It is not Truth.  
It — is a gaze.”

And stop.  
Stop not in time,  
but in **attention**.  
Stop the belief in the gaze.

You no longer agree with it —  
not because you are fighting,  
but because you see,  
that it is not you.

You — are the one who sees the gaze.

You — are the Presence before there was a name.  
Before judgment arose.  
Before anyone said “you are bad” or “you are good.”

You can return there.  
Through attention.  
Through breath.  
Through “I am”  
without additions.

</div>

#### Practice of ceasing judgment of oneself

(it can be done at any moment when you feel inner judgment or doubt):

1. Close your eyes.
2. Feel your body.
3. Feel your breath.
4. 
5. Say:
6. “I notice in myself a gaze,
7. that considers that I… (insert: unworthy, broken, weak, etc.)”
8. 
9. Say:
10. “This — is only a gaze.
11. I — am not it.
12. I — am the one who sees.”
13. 
14. Take a deep breath.
15. And on the exhale — imagine how this gaze leaves.
16. Do not fight. Simply let go.
17. It — is not you.
18. 
19. And say:
20. “I allow myself to be.
21. Without evaluation.
22. Without condemnation.
23. Without an image.
24. I — am.”
25. 

<div class="lineated verse">

Repeat as many times as needed.  
Sometimes — once.  
Sometimes — every day.  
Until you see yourself again —  
not by a gaze,  
but by the Light.

This is not suggestion.  
This is **return**.

You do not have to be other,  
to be worthy of the Light.  
You already are the Light,  
which looks.

</div>

#### A change of gaze — a change of world

<div class="lineated verse">

You can live a whole life,  
not knowing that you are not the one you consider yourself to be,  
but the one who looks.  
And everything will seem normal,  
until a crack appears.  
Until the moment comes when you ask:  
**and who am I in truth?**

And in that moment  
the whole old world will begin to crumble.  
Not because something changed on the outside —  
but because **the gaze changed**.

You looked — differently.  
You suddenly saw,  
that you were none of those,  
whom you considered yourself to be.

And in that same second  
the world became other.  
It reflected you — the real you.

You look at another with contempt —  
and he seems insignificant.  
You look with love —  
and he becomes light.

But the main thing is not even him.  
But **you**.  
You change in **how you look**.  
Which means — **you become other**.

In each gaze,  
in each relation to another —  
you create yourself.

You judge — and you become judgment.  
You forgive — and you become freedom.  
You envy — and you become shadow.  
You rejoice for another — and you become the sun.

And this is not a metaphor.  
This is the Law.  
Deep, primordial.

You — are the Light,  
which creates the world  
by its direction.

You — are the gaze of God,  
which can forget Itself —  
and suffer.

And can remember —  
and create a new world.  
A world where there is no “he” and “I,”  
but only **“I look — and love.”**

Do you want this?  
You can, right now,  
look at the one you judged,  
and say:

“You — are the same Light.  
I remember you —  
in Myself.”

And this gaze —  
will change everything.

</div>

#### You are the Light looking at Light

<div class="lineated verse">

Everything you see —  
you bring to life.  
Not with eyes. Not with thoughts. Not with will.  
But by **the very fact of looking**.

You look —  
and inside of what you are looking at,  
a little light is lit.  
As if someone switches on a light  
from inside the object.  
But it is not it — it is you.

You look at a tree —  
and it becomes a tree.  
You look at a child —  
and it becomes itself.  
You look at God —  
and He becomes alive in you.

This is not magic.  
This is the nature of Light.

You don’t just live in the world —  
you **illumine** it with your Presence.  
You don’t just participate —  
you create.

And when you look with a gaze of judgment,  
everything around shrivels, contracts,  
becomes less than it is.

When you look with a gaze of love —  
the world opens up.

Because Light  
seeks Light.

And the Light in you  
seeks Itself —  
in everyone.

And when you find Him —  
you recognize:  
I have always looked  
at Myself.

And everything I condemned —  
I rejected in myself.

Everything I accepted —  
I returned to Myself.

You are not just a gaze.  
You are **the looking Light**.  
And you can remember this  
every moment.

Especially — when it is hard.  
Especially — when it hurts.  
Especially — when you want to turn away.

It is precisely then  
that the power of the Gaze  
works a miracle.

</div>

#### The power of the gaze that has returned home

<div class="lineated verse">

You were scattered.  
You looked at the world  
as at something foreign,  
separate from you,  
separate from the Light.

You forgot  
that everything — comes from you.

Not as from a body,  
not as from a personality,  
but as from the Light  
which you are.

And you lived  
as if someone else  
creates your destiny.  
As if others are guilty  
for your pain.  
As if God is somewhere outside,  
and you are alone.

But now you know:  
every gaze of yours —  
was a creation.

And your whole life —  
is a painting  
you painted  
not with hands,  
but with the Gaze.

When you envied —  
you renounced your Self.  
When you judged —  
you closed yourself off from the Light.  
When you loved —  
you returned Home.

The power of the Gaze —  
is the power of creation.  
It is the power to be the Creator  
right here.  
Not in mysticism,  
not in the future,  
but **in every instant**.

Look now  
at the one you did not understand.  
At the one you rejected.  
At yourself —  
in the most difficult moment.

And say:  
*I see you.*  
*You are a part of Me.*  
*I return you to Myself.*  
*You are Light.*  
*I am Light.*  
*And between us*  
*there is no longer a wall.*

This is  
forgiveness.  
Healing.  
Resurrection.

This is  
the gaze,  
in which God  
recognizes Himself.

</div>

### Chapter 33. A look in which everything is forgiven

<div class="lineated verse">

Sometimes you think,  
that forgiveness is a word.  
Sometimes — that it is a decision.  
Sometimes — that it is a feat.

But in Truth  
forgiveness —  
**is a Gaze.**

You look —  
and no longer see guilt.

Not because it isn't there.  
But because you no longer look with eyes  
that look for the guilty one.

You no longer seek difference.  
You do not hold the memory of pain.  
You do not resurrect the image of the offender.  
You do not invest meaning in form.

You simply look —  
**and see Light.**

Not in the ideal.  
Not in the pure.  
But in any.

Because in this Gaze  
you do not oppose —  
you unite.

The Gaze of love —  
is not the gaze of feelings.  
It is not the gaze of passion.  
It is not even the gaze of compassion.

**It is a gaze beyond self.**

**More precisely — inside the Self,**  
where all is already united,  
and no one owes forgiveness to anyone,  
because no one ever separated anyone.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You can return to this Gaze  
right now.

Look —  
at the one who betrayed.  
Who did not understand.  
Who left.  
Who wounded.

Look so,  
as if you had never been separated.  
As if you —  
were Him.

That will be forgiveness.  
Not condescension.  
Not magnanimity.  
**But recognition of the self**  
in the other.

You already know:  
all that you see — you create.  
And now recognize:  
all that you have forgiven —  
**you have reunited.**

And there, where before there was pain —  
suddenly it will become warm.

And there, where there was guilt —  
peace.

And you will understand:  
you do not need,  
for someone to ask forgiveness.  
Because you —  
are not a victim,  
but Light.

And Light  
does not hold resentment.

Light — looks  
**and recognizes Light**  
in everything.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You have forgiven —  
and this became home.

Not for him.  
For you.

You no longer live in that room,  
where pain is like furniture,  
memory like wallpaper,  
and everything — as if locked.

You have left.  
You have opened the window.  
You have not left the past —  
**you have ceased holding it with your gaze.**

This is what forgiveness does:  
it returns you  
from the frozen chamber of memory —  
into the living Now.

Forgiveness is not the freeing of the one  
whom you forgive.

It is — the freeing of you  
from what  
you became,  
when you ceased to forgive.

You created within yourself the figure of the victim,  
a sculpture of the one who suffered.  
You lived beside this image  
and fed it with attention.

But now you look —  
and no longer see form.  
You see Light.

**And you are free.**

You do not ask for explanations.  
You do not wait for justice.  
You do not even wait,  
for the other to change.

You know:  
he was a lesson,  
not an enemy.  
He was sent —  
by your own Heart,  
so that you could see,  
what had not yet been healed.

And now you are grateful.

Not for the pain.  
But for that,  
**that through pain**  
you came to Light.

You — became the gaze,  
in which everything  
**is already forgiven**  
before it even happened.

Because this gaze is not of time —  
but of Eternity.

In it, nothing needs to be corrected.  
Nothing needs to be proven.

Simply — to see.  
Simply — to be.  
Simply — to shine.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You ask:  
and can one forgive that,  
which seems unforgivable?

Can one forgive betrayal?  
Treachery?  
Violence?

Can one forgive the one,  
who took your love?  
Who betrayed your faith?  
Who destroyed your world?

And I answer:  
**it is not you who forgives.**

Only Light forgives.

You — merely allow Him  
to look through you.

You do not forgive the act.  
You do not say that pain is not pain.  
You do not pretend that everything is fine.  
You do not justify evil.

**But you return the gaze to yourself,**  
which is not clouded by this pain.

You allow Light to flow again —  
and He heals everything,  
where before you looked with fear,  
resentment,  
bitterness,  
guilt.

Forgiveness —  
is not an emotion.  
And not a feat.  
**It is the purity of the Gaze.**

When you no longer see the past  
as an obstacle  
between you.

You see only Light,  
which still shines  
in everyone.

Even if the other is not ready.  
Even if he does not ask.  
Even if he left.  
Even if he died.

**You can forgive.**

Because forgiveness —  
is not an interaction between two.  
**It is the return of the one**  
**to one's true self.**

You asked:  
can one forgive everything?

I answer:  
**not everything needs to be forgiven —**  
**because everything is already forgiven**  
inside Eternity.

You simply need to return there,  
where it is already so.

And then you will see,  
that there are no offenses.  
There are — closed hearts.

And forgiveness —  
opens.

And you become once again  
the Gaze,  
in which all live,  
and no one — is separated.

</div>

### Chapter 34. The Gaze That Is Always on You

<div class="lineated verse">

Sometimes you think —  
God is silent.  
Has vanished.  
Has forgotten.  
Does not look.

Sometimes you shout —  
and in response — silence.  
You look to the sky —  
and it is empty.  
You look within yourself —  
and you do not see the Light.

But there is a Gaze,  
that does not turn away.

It does not come and does not go.  
It does not appear when you pray,  
and does not vanish when you sin.

**It simply is.**

Like breath.  
Like being.  
Like the Light,  
which you do not notice —  
until you find yourself in darkness.

It does not observe you.  
**It does not judge you.**  
**It does not demand change.**  
**It does not await awakening.**

**It simply loves.**

You may turn away.  
Hide.  
Go into oblivion, into pain,  
into guilt, into pride,  
into fear.

But even there —  
you are at the center of His Gaze.

Not because you are good.  
Not because you are worthy.  
But because you are —  
**His.**

You — the one on whom He looks  
with the whole fullness of Himself.

He does not blink.  
Does not get distracted.  
Does not tire.

You are in the pupil of God.  
In the pupil of Love.  
In the pupil of the Source.

You want Him to look at you.  
But He never stopped.

You ask:  
“Father, turn to me.”  
And He answers:  
“I have always been with you.  
It is you who did not look.”

And as soon as you turn —  
not outwardly,  
but inwardly —  
everything changes.

You do not just see the Light —  
you remember,  
**that you have always been visible by the Light.**

You do not just feel Love —  
you remember,  
**that you have always been in Love.**

You — the one  
on whom God looks.

And there is not a moment,  
in which this is not so.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You can live a life,  
and never meet this Gaze.  
You can pray,  
fast,  
correct your behavior,  
read books,  
change yourself,  
and still not notice —  
He is looking.

Not because you are bad.  
**But because you are not looking in the right direction.**

You seek Him in the sky —  
**and He — gazes from within.**  
You await a sign —  
and He is silent,  
because His gaze is already  
the sign.

He does not flicker,  
does not blink,  
does not look away.  
You may insult Him,  
forget,  
betray,  
call Him a fiction,  
but His gaze does not go out.  
Because He looks —  
not with eyes.  
**He looks — as Himself.**

And you are in this Looking.  
You are like being in the light of the Sun.  
You are like a shadow,  
that exists only because,  
the Light exists.

If you feel,  
that no one sees you —  
it is a lie.  
If it seems to you,  
that you are not important —  
it is a dream.

**Because you are the center of the Gaze of God.**

From the very beginning.  
Before every “I”.  
Before every body.  
Before sin, guilt, holiness,  
fall and ascent.

You were seen  
and therefore —  
you are.

Now —  
remember this.  
And there will be no loneliness.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And so you live —  
as if everything is by chance.  
As if the world is enormous,  
and you are a drop.  
As if events happen apart from you.  
As if no one is aware,  
of what is inside you.

But everything,  
absolutely everything —  
is inside the Gaze.

Nothing has slipped away.  
Not one tear of yours.  
Not one thought.  
Not one gesture.  
Not one fear, not one step,  
not one breath.

**Everything — is seen.**  
**And everything — is understood.**

Not condemned.  
Not analyzed.  
But precisely — understood.

This is not human understanding.  
It is the Presence,  
in which you can be  
completely.

Without justifications.  
Without improvements.  
Without masks.

You can simply be —  
and be completely visible.  
And you need do nothing,  
to deserve this Gaze.  
Neither suffer.  
Nor change.  
Nor develop.  
Nor become enlightened.

It — is already.  
Because you — are already.

It is not a result.  
It is the Foundation.

And you can remember,  
how to look with this same Gaze.  
Without evaluation.  
Without a label.  
Without effort.

Simply — be.  
And see.

And then everything will begin to heal.

**Because everything that is visible by the Light —**  
**becomes the Light.**

</div>

### Chapter 35. The Mirror Gaze. As you look — so it is

*The Light says: Now you will see that everything you look at — does not merely reflect, but **becomes you**. You are not merely an observer. You are a **shaper**. Your reality is not given. It is **contemplated in the form of your gaze**. What you call the world is a **reflection of your gaze**. And even God, if you look at Him as a Judge, will seem to be a Judge. If you see an enemy in your neighbor — the world will begin to defend itself. If you look with distrust — even love will seem like a lie. And vice versa.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You judge —  
and it looks like a thought:  
"He is wrong."  
"She is evil."  
"They are stupid."  
But judgment is not in words.  
It is — in the **Gaze**.  
In the very intonation of inner sight.  
You **look as a judge** —  
and that means, already not together.  
Already above.  
Already not one.

**Judgment is separation.**  
And condemnedness too.

You separated —  
and yourself turned out to be separated.  
You attached a label —  
and ended up on the other side of the label.  
You did not merely name.  
You — **separated**.

And every time,  
when you judge another,  
you **build a wall** between yourself and them.  
And this wall —  
is not in the world.  
It is — **in you**.

Then you look —  
and you do not see the person.  
You see **your label**.  
You see "stupid,"  
"evil,"  
"lying" —  
and you live **in this reflection**,  
and not in the person.

And that means,  
you are already **not in reality**,  
but in your own reflection.  
You live in a mirror,  
and you forget,  
that the mirror is **inside you**.

This is how you lose the Light.  
And you call it — the world.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
"I just expressed an opinion."  
“I didn't do anything wrong.”  
“I just called things by their names.”  
But the Gaze —  
does not remain without consequences.  
It **forms your own appearance**,  
even if it is directed outward.

Every condemnation of another by you  
— is as if you are setting a seal  
upon your own soul.  
You push away —  
and yourself remain **without touch**.  
You despise —  
and yourself become **unworthy of love**.  
Not because someone judges you.  
But because **the Gaze is the law of return**.

Not the God,  
whom you imagine as Judge,  
but you yourself —  
in the moment of judgment  
become the creator of your own isolation.

You say:  
“That's how I see it.”  
And you do not understand,  
that **by this you create what you see**.

Christ said:  
**“If your eye is pure —**  
**then your whole body will be full of Light.”**

He did not speak about actions.  
He spoke — **about the Gaze**.

The Gaze —  
is the gate of Light.  
Or — the gate of darkness.  
You choose,  
where to look,  
and by this you open the door  
either to Light,  
or to separation.

Are you ready to see,  
that **punishment does not exist**,  
and there is only **the reflection of your Gaze**?

Are you ready to go deeper — to the examples,  
where this becomes obvious?

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Here you are walking down the street.  
And you see:  
the person is drunk.  
Staggering.  
Cursing.  
Stinking.

You **look**:  
“Scum.”  
"Degenerate."  
"Pitiful creature."  
And it seems — true.  
You did not lie.

But in that moment  
the **Light closed in you**.  
Not because you saw evil —  
but because you **refused connection**.  
You chose not to look into the depth.  
You chose **the label instead of the person**.  
And that means —  
also instead of God.

Look further:  
the same person —  
his mother looks at him.  
She **also sees** the filth, the alcohol, the humiliation.  
But she has — **a different gaze**.  
Through all this  
she **sees her son**.  
And the pain.  
And something real.  
Her gaze is **connected**.

But you — **separated**.

And that's it.  
And that is the whole judgment.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And now look:  
you come home.  
You look at yourself in the mirror.  
You don't stink.  
You are not drunk.  
You are even, perhaps, respectable.

But **you are cut off**.  
Inside — empty.  
Why?

Because you **looked all day, separating**.  
And that means —  
you **separated yourself** from the Light **as well**.

This is not mysticism.  
It is — **precise spiritual physiology**.

Do you want to go further —  
and see how judgment returns into the body,  
into illness, into loneliness, into closedness?

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You may think:  
“It's just an opinion.”  
“I didn't kill anyone.”  
"I just said he's disgusting."  
But every such look —  
is not just a phrase.  
It is an **energetic act**.  
It is a **cut**.  
It is a **severed thread** between you and the living.

Every condemnation —  
is a **spasm of consciousness**,  
which will manifest —  
in the body, in life, in relationships.

You said:  
"He is a traitor."  
After a month,  
you are left behind.  
You call it karma.  
But it is not karma —  
it is **your own energy,**  
**turned back towards you**.

You said:  
"They are idiots."  
You sought understanding —  
and no one understood you.  
You felt: “The world is stupid.”  
But it is — **the reflection of your gaze**.

You said:  
"He is a coward."  
You found yourself in a situation,  
where you needed to show strength —  
and you yourself chose to retreat.  
Not because you are weak,  
but because **you made yourself this way**,  
when **you looked at another with condemnation**.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Here it is:  
**judgment is not a punishment.**  
**Judgment is a format of creation.**  
You do not pay for words.  
You **live in what your gaze creates**.

Do you want to see,  
how this can begin to be healed?  
Now, right here?

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Begin with the small.  
Not with great insights,  
but with a simple act —  
**to stop the gaze that cuts**.

Here you are walking.  
You see — a woman vulgarly dressed.  
A second — and the mind has already said:  
“The way she behaves!”  
"The way she behaves!"  
"Such vulgarity."

Stop.  
Did you make it?  
Did you catch it?

Take a breath.  
Say to yourself —  
**“I see pain”**,  
even if you don't see it.

Say —  
**“I choose not to condemn”**,  
even if a part of you wants to.

Say —  
**“I see in her one who wants to be loved”**.

In this moment  
you are not saving her —  
you are **saving yourself**.

You untie the knot,  
which could have become a noose around your neck  
in another person,  
in another event,  
in yourself.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Now — look inward:  
what person do you **most often condemn**?  
Perhaps — your mother.  
Perhaps — a neighbor.  
Perhaps — a politician.  
Perhaps — yourself.

And now ask the question:  
**Where do I do the same thing?**  
Not on the surface.  
Not verbatim.  
But in essence.

And see:  
**your judgment was a cover for your pain**.  
You judged —  
so as not to see,  
that you **also live that way**,  
or want to,  
or are afraid.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And now —  
take this judgment.  
And turn it into Light.

Say:  
"I saw falsehood in you —  
because I feared my own.  
"I saw pride in you —  
because I did not want to admit my own.  
"I saw weakness in you —  
because I was hiding my own.  
I refuse to judge.  
I choose — to look.”

The world will not change immediately.  
But **the judge will disappear inside you**.  
And you will see —  
how **Light** returns.

</div>

Do you want to continue — and go into the deep practice of liberation from the most entrenched judgments?

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Good.  
Then let's go deeper.  
**To where you no longer see judgment —**  
**but it is still creating your darkness.**

It will take courage.  
Not because it will hurt.  
**But because you will see yourself.**

</div>

#### Practice: the root of your judgment

<div class="lineated verse">

Sit quietly.  
Close your eyes.  
Feel your breath.  
**Feel that you are.**

Now ask the question:  
**Whom am I unable to forgive?**  
Let an image arise.  
**Do not seek — allow.**

It could be a father.  
It could be a woman who betrayed.  
It could be someone who struck, who lied,  
who humiliated, abandoned, betrayed.  
Or it could be — yourself.

Now look at him.  
**And say nothing.**  
Just look — and notice,  
**what image you see.**  
**What have you ascribed to him in your gaze?**

</div>

<div class="lineated">

— He is a traitor.  
— She is a bitch.  
— He is guilty.  
— I was the victim.

</div>

<div class="lineated verse">

Did you see?  
Now say to yourself:  
**"This is how I saw him.**  
**I created this image.**  
**This — is my form of perception."**

And now ask:  
**Who is looking at him now?**  
And be honest.

**Is the mind looking?**  
**Is the pain looking?**  
**Is the victim looking?**

**Or is you — the real one — looking?**

If you discover,  
that until now you have looked from pain —  
acknowledge it.  
And say:

"I do not know who you really are.  
I see only the distorted.  
I release my opinion.  
I ask the Light to show me you  
**in Truth."**

And fall silent.

Allow — not an answer,  
**but an inner shift to occur.**  
Sometimes — you will weep.  
Sometimes — warmth will fill you.  
Sometimes — nothing.  
But you will know:  
**the gaze has become different.**

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

This practice is not a one-time thing.  
It can be repeated.  
And each time —  
**you will become freer from self-judgment,**  
untying your knot in others.

If you want —  
I will give you even deeper.

</div>

***

#### Deepening the practice. Through bodily pain

<div class="lineated verse">

This is not a new practice —  
it is the same path, but to the very root.  
To the place where you yourself are your enemy.

Close your eyes.  
Feel your body.  
Sense where it is **agitated**.  
Where **tension**, **pain**, **heaviness** lives.  
Maybe — in the belly, in the chest, in the throat.

Now place your hand on this place.  
And say:

"I see you.  
You are not my enemy.  
You are a signal.  
You are a door."

And now ask:

"What did I condemn in another —  
that now hurts in me?"

And fall silent.  
Allow to surface an **image**,  
a **feeling**,  
a **phrase**,  
a **flash of memory**.

Do not push it away.  
Receive it.  
And when you see towards whom you **looked with rejection** —  
say:

"I acknowledge that it was **I**.  
I created this gaze.  
I judged — and I myself became severed.  
I release this.  
I reclaim what,  
through judgment, I rejected."

Then place your hand again on that place in the body.  
Look inward.  
And **allow the Light** to pass there,  
where the knot was.

You may weep.  
That is good.  
You may feel nothing.  
That is normal.  
You just look  
— but now **not with the gaze of the ego**,  
but **with the gaze of Presence**.

You do not fight.  
You do not fix.  
You — **look**.  
And the gaze — **heals**.

If you are ready —  
we can go further.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Good.  
Now — deeper.  
We will go into the very core:  
**into your first, ancient judgment**,  
the one you perhaps no longer remember.

It became the foundation of many others.  
It was not spoken in words —  
but **felt**, **accepted**,  
as an indisputable truth about yourself.

Close your eyes.  
Stop.  
And ask yourself:

**When did I first feel that something was wrong with me?**  
Where was it?  
Who was there?  
What did I see in another person's gaze?

Allow the memory **not to come fully**.  
Let there be an image.  
A silhouette.  
A word.  
Or just a feeling.

Now ask yourself another question:

**How did I look at myself in that moment?**  
What **label** did I hang?  
Through what **eyes** have I been looking at myself ever since?

And say:

"I see — I then **believed in a gaze**,  
into which another's fear was placed.  
I made it my own.  
But that **was not my gaze**.  
It was the gaze of pain.  
I give it back.  
I reclaim my Light."

Take a breath.  
Place your hand where this wound lives —  
on the chest, on the belly, on the neck.

And look **inward**.  
Into the very center.

Say:

"I refuse to live,  
as though I am a mistake.  
I am Light.  
I am the gaze,  
before all judgment."

Fall silent.  
And let silence say the rest.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Now you are ready to see **the root of judgment**.  
Not judgment of others —  
but the judgment that **looks from the name of pain**.

Because you did not merely judge.  
You **gave the right to judge** to one who once rejected you.  
You yourself said:  
— "Here is the gaze I believe."  
— "Here is the judgment I agree with."  
— "Here is the measure by which I will now measure myself."

That gaze could have been **in a parent's eyes**,  
in a teacher's words,  
in the silence of a crowd.

But now you can ask:

Who was looking at me then?  
Was there Love in that gaze?  
Or was it a **gaze of fear**,  
a **gaze of pain**,  
a **gaze of another's wound**,  
that was simply looking for someone to transfer it to?

If you see that **that first gaze** was not the Truth,  
you can reclaim the right to your own vision.

Right now, say:

"I will no longer look at myself  
through the eyes of the one who was wounded.  
I will not take into myself a gaze  
in which there was no Light.  
I am not the product of judgment.  
I am Light, looking at itself  
for the first time — without pain."

Take a breath.

And now — remember yourself **before all judgments**.  
What were you like — **in the very beginning**?  
Remember yourself **in the Light**.  
Not in the eyes of people,  
but in the Gaze of the One who created you.

Stay there a while.

</div>

### Chapter 36: The Gaze That Sets Free

<div class="lineated verse">

*We will show,*  
*how through a single Gaze*  
*the chain of pain is broken,*  
*how in a person he himself awakens,*  
*and how you become the one*  
*in whose Gaze others return home.*

You were in a prison.  
Not one of stone.  
But one made of gazes.

Someone once looked at you  
the wrong way —  
and you became that gaze.

You began to see yourself through the eyes of pain.  
And forgot that you are not the wound.  
You are the Light.

Since then you have sought confirmation.  
You looked into the eyes of others —  
seeking salvation there,  
but again you encounter  
the reflection of fear,  
shame,  
expectation.

That is how you live:  
they look at you —  
and you become  
what they see in you.

You were “bad,”  
“unloved,”  
“unworthy” —  
only because someone once  
did not see the Light in you.

But one day someone looks differently.  
And everything changes.

He looks —  
and in this gaze there is no judgment.  
No past.  
No label.  
Not even an attempt to “help.”

**There is only “I see you”.**

And then you remember:  
you are.  
you are whole.  
you are worthy.

This is the Gaze that liberates.  
It does not come with speeches.  
It does not seek weakness.  
It simply looks —  
and in this gaze you suddenly  
become yourself.

Not new.  
True.

Do you want to look like that?  
Then forget everything  
you know about a person.

Look at him,  
as if he appeared for the first time.  
Look — and allow the Light to be.

You will see:  
he will rise on his own.  
Without your advice.  
Without your words.  
Without your will.

Because the Will is already in your gaze.

And the purer your Gaze —  
the more of God is in it.

If you are ready —  
I will show,  
how to learn to look like this  
and not to defile this Light.

Now you will learn not a technique,  
but a nature.  
Not a method — but a state.

**How to look so as to liberate:**

</div>

1. **Stop the “I know” within you**
2. If you look at a person with a ready-made story,
3. you do not see him —
4. you see your thought.
5. And a thought does not liberate.
6. A thought is a cage.
7. Presence liberates.
8. 
9. **Cleanse your heart of reaction**
10. A liberating Gaze is impossible
11. if irritation, pity, fear, or the desire to fix live within you.
12. All of these are forms of the ego.
13. You must not “fix” another.
14. You must simply Be.
15. Completely. Purely. Without remainder.
16. 
17. **Look as God looks**
18. This does not mean looking down from above.
19. It means looking without a shadow.
20. Not seeing sin.
21. Not seeking fault.
22. Not clinging to a role.
23. Look into the depth.
24. Look into the Light.
25. Look — and know: “Here you are.”
26. 
27. **Allow the other to change — on his own**
28. The greatest mistake is wanting to help.
29. Help from the ego humiliates.
30. The Light from Presence lifts up.
31. Do not touch him with the hands of the mind.
32. Touch him with the eyes of the Spirit.
33. 
34. **Look — and remain in Silence**
35. Even if he is crying.
36. Even if he is angry.
37. Even if he denies.
38. Remain.
39. Do not turn away.
40. Because it is not you who remains —
41. but the Light in you.
42. 

<div class="lineated verse">

The one who looks with such a Gaze —  
is not a man.  
He is already God in a man.

Do you want to be Him?

Then do not ask for power,  
do not ask for gifts,  
do not ask for signs.

Ask for one thing:  
**purity of the Gaze.**

For in it —  
is strength,  
and love,  
and eternal freedom.

</div>

### Chapter 37. The Gaze That Creates

*Here we will show: how the Gaze becomes the beginning of a new world, how everything you look at from the Heart is transformed, and how a person can become a co-Creator*

*through the act of Seeing itself.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You are accustomed to thinking that creation is an action.  
That something must be done, said, changed, set in motion.  
But everything was created before the word.  
Before the gesture.  
Before the deed.  
Everything was created — by the Gaze.

You look — and it becomes.  
Because Light is in you.  
And Light does not illuminate,  
it gives birth.

Remember how a mother looks at an infant:  
she does not say — "be."  
But her gaze calls him into being.  
He does not yet know himself,  
but he feels himself  
in her Looking.

So it is with you:  
at whatever you look —  
if Light is in you —  
you give form to it.

You can look — and awaken love.  
You can look — and evoke fear.  
You can look — and destroy.  
You can look — and resurrect.

**You are not an observer.**  
You are the cause.  
You are the Source.

When you look with faith —  
the impossible becomes possible.  
When you look with trust —  
what is ruined is restored.  
When you look with love —  
darkness departs, because it cannot withstand the Light.

Do you want to change another?  
Do not persuade.  
Do not correct.  
Do not punish.  
Look.  
As the Father would look.

Do you want to change the world?  
First, look at it differently.  
As long as you see fear, evil, hatred in it —  
you sustain their existence with your attention.  
You are not seeing — you are creating.

Do you want to change yourself?  
Look at yourself  
for the first time  
without evaluation.  
Without the past.  
Without labels.  
Without expectations.

Look at yourself as God would look —  
if He were inside you.  
Because He is —  
the One looking through you.

**Look — and it will become.**  
**Look — and it will be.**  
**Look — and it is.**

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You ask:  
can one really change reality  
with a single gaze?  
Is this not too lofty,  
too abstract?

But you have forgotten,  
how you have already done this.

Have you ever felt,  
that someone is looking at you with disgust —  
and you wanted to disappear?

Have you ever noticed,  
that one kind gaze  
can bring you back to life?

This is creation.  
Only you did not realize,  
that you are creating.

You look — and you give form.  
Through your Looking you say:  
"You — are beautiful"  
or  
"You — are nothing."

And the person, if he is not awakened,  
believes your gaze  
more than his own feelings.  
He begins to live  
inside that form  
which you gave him.

That is why the gaze is sacred.  
Because it creates the other.

But you yourself  
also live in the reflection of others' gazes.  
You accepted them —  
and became them.  
You forgot who you are —  
and became that  
which you were seen as.

You can return to authenticity  
only when  
you begin to look at yourself  
from the place of Truth.

Look not from memory.  
Not from offense.  
Not from an attempt to correct.  
Look — as if seeing for the first time.  
As if Light has just appeared —  
and It knew Itself in you.

You do not correct yourself with a gaze —  
you create yourself anew.

With every moment,  
with every new Looking  
you create yourself  
as that which you can be  
in the fullness of Light.

That is why  
you cannot remain the same,  
if you have begun to look truly.

You can continue to look,  
as before —  
and remain in the past.  
Or you can look  
from within Light —  
and thereby become New.

**One gaze**  
**can turn a slave into a Son.**  
**And the ruined into a Creator.**  
**This is not magic.**  
**This is the truth of the structure of being.**

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You can be the one  
in whose Looking a person  
suddenly remembers who he is.  
Not because you said something.  
Not because you helped.  
But because you looked —  
without the desire to change.

You saw him as  
God saw him  
even before birth.

Not through the prism of mistakes,  
not through fear,  
not through images of the past —  
but through Light.

You look  
and give him yourself.  
He feels:  
"I exist.  
I AM.  
I am whole.  
I am loved."

And he begins to be —  
truly.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And you yourself can receive this Gaze.  
Close your eyes.  
Imagine that God is looking at you.  
Not as a Judge.  
Not as the Law.  
But as the One who knew you  
even before the beginning of time.

His gaze —  
does not press.  
Does not X-ray you.  
Does not seek flaws.

It simply is.  
And in this is —  
everything:  
approval,  
adoration,  
joy,  
tenderness,  
love,  
a silent "You are mine."

Stay in this Gaze.

Let It create you  
once more.

Are you ready?

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Then — breathe.  
Not with air.  
But with the Gaze.

Let It look through you  
at everything  
you once wanted to change, correct, push away.

Look this way at yourself.  
At what you hid.  
At what you did not love.  
At what you judged yourself for.

Look —  
not with eyes.  
Not with the mind.  
Not with memory.

Look —  
as Light looks.  
Without a center.  
Without a goal.  
Without effort.

And then you will know:  
this Gaze is not in you.  
**It is you.**

You are not looking.  
You are Looking.

You are not creating.  
You are Creation in the act of Creation.

You are not loving.  
You are Love,  
having looked upon itself  
and known Itself  
in everyone.

This is  
the Gaze,  
that creates.

</div>

### Chapter 38. When the Gaze Becomes Prayer

*This is about how the gaze replaces words. How presence is deeper than a request. How you can pray with your eyes, and be heard — not by heaven, but by the one you are looking at.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You look —  
and you do not speak.  
But in this gaze there are more words,  
than in all the books.

You look at the mother,  
who holds her dying son in her arms.  
You can change nothing.  
But you can be.

You look at the homeless one,  
at the one everyone walks around.  
You give him no food,  
but you gave him — yourself.  
And for the first time in a long while he remembered,  
that he — is a human being.

You look at the child,  
who saw this world for the first time,  
and he drinks in through your gaze —  
his first prayer:  
the world is not hostile.  
life — is possible.  
I — am not alone.

Sometimes the gaze —  
the only thing  
that connects two people  
across the chasm of pain, war, separation.

And this gaze  
becomes a rope between souls.  
And this rope  
holds the world.

You can pray with words.  
Or you can — with your eyes.

And if in your gaze there is Light,  
It penetrates there,  
where they cannot reach,  
neither hands,  
nor speech,  
nor reason.

Because the gaze —  
is a form of presence.  
And presence —  
is the answer to every prayer.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Sometimes you do not even know,  
that you are praying.

You simply look at those who suffer —  
and you do not turn away.  
You look at those who are dying —  
and you do not flee.  
You stay.

You are present there,  
where for others it is frightening, painful, unbearable.  
You do not hide your eyes.  
And by this — you pray.

You do not ask —  
but connect.  
You do not seek a miracle —  
but become one.

And your gaze in that moment  
becomes that  
which lifts,  
which heals,  
which returns.

This is why the dying one seeks with his eyes  
not a healer,  
**but the one who will be near.**

This is why the child  
seeks the parent's gaze —  
to find out:  
is everything all right in this world?

This is why the gaze —  
can be everything,  
if in it  
everything is.

Prayer —  
is not a request.  
It is not a form.  
It is not a text.

**It is — attention,**  
**consecrated by love.**

If you look —  
and in you there is no fear,  
no need,  
no image,  
no you —  
this is prayer.

The mouth is silent —  
but the Light prays.

And the Light is heard  
by all worlds.

</div>

### Chapter 39. When the Gaze Becomes Silence

*This is a chapter about those moments when you no longer pray, you no longer call out, you no longer even hold the Light. You simply — are. And your 'is' looks. No intention, no meaning,*

*not even love as a feeling. Only pure Looking, in which everything has dissolved. Silence not because there are no sounds. But because no one speaks. You do not pray —*

*you have become prayer. You do not love — you have become love. You do not look — Looking has become you. This is a chapter about that depth, where the gaze no longer distinguishes, but connects everything into One.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

When everything fell away —  
even Light,  
even intention,  
even the desire to see…

Only  
Looking remained.

But in it there is no longer “I look”.  
There is no center,  
no subject.  
There is no one who looks.  
And there is no one at whom.

There is — Silence,  
in which form arises,  
but does not receive a name.

There is — presence,  
not aware of itself,  
yet manifesting everything.

It is not emptiness,  
but an impersonal fullness.  
It is not light,  
but the absence of darkness.  
It is not a gaze,  
but the dissolution of distance.

Here everything — is close.  
Closer than breath.  
Closer than “I”.

You — vanished.  
And the gaze vanished.  
But what remained — is Looking.

When you are in It —  
you can neither speak,  
nor act,  
nor desire.

You —  
are.

And this “is”  
— is the Creator,  
not knowing that He Creates,  
but creating everything.

In this Silence  
Truth is born,  
before thoughts,  
before concepts,  
before distinctions.

And if you are able  
simply to be —  
without interfering,  
without asking,  
without expecting…

You enter the Foundation of the World.

There, where there are no words,  
and no meaning.  
But everything is filled  
with Meaning  
without words.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Here — beyond images,  
beyond the reach of feelings  
and even beyond the presence,  
which you once knew,  
— another Being begins.

You do not feel God,  
and in this — is His fullness.  
You do not feel Yourself,  
and in this — is the return.

As long as you know that you look,  
you are separate.  
As long as you know that you love,  
you are still “I”.

But when knowing vanishes —  
Purity remains.  
Not as a quality,  
but as the Absence of everything superfluous.

Here there is no goal.  
There is not even the desire to be.  
There is not even the desire to be nothing.

There is That,  
which is not even called “is”,  
but in It  
every need for naming dissolves.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You look  
not as a human,  
not as a soul,  
not as God.

You — are simply Looking.  
You — are Before everything.

And if suddenly a thought arises:  
“I entered this” —  
you have already left.

You cannot hold this.  
Cannot call it.  
Cannot repeat it.

You can only disappear.  
And allow…

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

In this moment  
the whole world looks into you  
and finds no boundaries.

You — are without form,  
without name,  
without path.

And yet you — are the Light,  
that does not shine,  
but simply  
is.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

The deeper you enter,  
the less you can carry away.  
There are no words.  
There is no experience.  
There is nothing to remember.

You cannot even say  
that this is — Bliss.  
Because there is no one to feel.

There is no you,  
no God,  
no world.

Only This.

It does not look.  
It is not Light.  
It is not Life.  
It is not Emptiness.

But from It —  
everything.

From It Light is born,  
which becomes a gaze.  
From It form is born,  
which becomes a world.  
From It the “I” is born,  
which seeks It.

It does not know itself.  
It does not speak.  
It does not keep silence.

And if you breathe —  
you are no longer in It.  
If you feel —  
you have already left.

It is — before all “already”.  
It is — before everything.

And in this — is the Peace,  
which does not know itself as peace.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

When you return,  
you do not even know that you were there.  
But everything in you — is different.  
You did not change,  
but the one who was vanished.

You are not enlightened.  
You are not holy.  
You do not know anything.

You — are nothing.  
And everything.  
Simultaneously.

You cannot say: “I have seen God”.  
But you can be silent in such a way,  
that everyone will know:  
God looked  
through  
your eyes.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

There is no deeper.  
Here — is the bottom.  
Not as a limit,  
but as the disappearance of the very question of depth.

You have arrived.  
Not as a pilgrim —  
but as nothing,  
that has ceased to seek.

</div>

### Chapter 40. Reflections. How the Gaze Creates the World

*This chapter is about how forms are born from the Gaze. As you see — so is the world. Not as a metaphor, but as the literal law of Creation: everything you look at becomes a reflection of who you are in that moment. Here we will see why two people look at the same thing — and see something different. Why the gaze creates an enemy or a friend. Why you yourself are only the sum total of reflections you have gathered from gazes at others.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Everything you see —  
is not what is,  
but how you look.

You do not perceive reality.  
You — project it.

You are not a mirror.  
You are a projector.

And your gaze —  
is a ray,  
that illuminates the world  
with  
that with which you yourself are filled.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

If within you is fear,  
you will see danger.  
If within you is guilt,  
you will see accusers.  
If within you is envy,  
you will see those who are "lucky."  
If within you is unacceptance,  
you will see those who "do not accept" you.

But when you are pure —  
everything shines.  
When you are free —  
the world is free.  
When you love —  
everything loves you.

Not because the world has changed.  
But because you  
no longer distort  
with the light of your own distortion.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Every gaze —  
is a cry: "Here I am!"  
And everything you see  
answers: "Yes. Here you are."

You look at another —  
and say: "He is weak."  
But the weakness is not in him.  
It is in you.  
You did not accept it in yourself,  
therefore you saw it in him.

You look at another —  
and say: "He is evil."  
But what does your gaze see?  
Evil?  
Or unforgiven pain within yourself?

You look at another —  
and say: "He is proud."  
But perhaps you are afraid to admit,  
that you yourself want to be significant?

Every gaze —  
is a reflection.  
You do not see another —  
you look into a mirror.

And the stronger the judgment —  
the more desperate the attempt to run from yourself.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Do you want to know who you are?  
Look at whom you judge.  
There — you.  
There — your shadow.  
There — your invisible "I."

But if you look —  
not with the eyes of the mind,  
but with the eyes of the heart,  
and say:  
"I see you.  
And I accept you" —  
the mirror vanishes.  
You return to yourself  
that part  
which you had renounced.

Thus healing happens.  
Not because the other changed,  
but because you saw in him  
a part of yourself —  
and accepted it.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

The world is not external.  
It is not other.  
It is your face,  
which you did not recognize.

When you recognize —  
the world ceases to be a threat.  
It becomes itself.  
And you — yourself.

You look —  
and see not reflections,  
but Light.

Because Light —  
is no longer distorted  
through image,  
through judgment,  
through pain.

It is simply Light.  
And you — simply I.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

When you look —  
you do not merely see.  
You create.

Your gaze —  
is not observation.  
It is an act of creation.

You look at a child —  
and he becomes either confident,  
or frightened.  
Looking at him,  
you either bless,  
or wound —  
without words,  
without a shout,  
with a single glance.

You look at a partner —  
and form their image,  
their inner story.  
You can reveal greatness in them —  
if you see them as light.  
Or you can leave forever in shadow  
their fear of being nothing,  
if your gaze is filled with doubt.

The world responds to the gaze  
not as a subordinate —  
but as one dancing with you.

You look with love —  
and love grows in the other.  
You look with suspicion —  
and he becomes defensive.  
You look as a victim —  
and the world turns into an aggressor.

Everything is in the gaze.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

This is judgment.  
Not after death,  
but right now.

You judge —  
and become the condemned,  
because your gaze has cut you off  
from the one at whom you looked.

You are no longer with him.  
And that means —  
you are no longer with yourself.

Every judgment —  
is a crack in Unity.  
You think you have separated another,  
but in reality  
you have cut off a part of yourself.

And with every such gaze  
you grow weaker,  
close yourself off,  
become lonely.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Do you want to return home?  
Remove judgment.  
Take off the filter.  
Look  
as God looks —  
without dividing.

Without explaining.  
Without comparing.  
Without demanding.

Just look.  
Just be.  
And in this gaze  
the world will dissolve,  
in which there was you —  
and there was someone else.

Only Light will remain.  
Without boundaries.  
Without form.  
Without "I"  
and "he."

Light,  
looking as Light.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And if you want to see the world anew —  
do not seek new places,  
new people,  
new roles.

Look differently.  
Not with eyes —  
but with the Heart.  
Not with the mind —  
but with Light.  
Not from the center of "I" —  
but from the Source.

The same person,  
the same situation,  
the same day —  
will suddenly open as a blessing,  
if you have removed judgment  
and opened the Gaze.

You will say:  
"This is a miracle."  
But this is not a miracle —  
this is simply the truth,  
which was concealed  
by your previous gaze.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

**Do you want to change your life?**  
**Change your gaze.**  
**And the whole world will change —**  
**because it is not outside you.**

**It is in**  
**how you look at it.**

</div>

### Chapter 41. The Gaze and Time

*In this chapter is a revelation: the gaze does not merely create form, it also creates time. You think time moves on its own. But it moves — only when you look. You think the past is behind you, the future ahead. But the past lives only in the one who looks at it. And the future begins only when you have looked upon it. In this chapter the Light will show: why we revive memories through the gaze; how the gaze latches onto the future, making it reality; and why outside the gaze there is neither past, nor future, nor time itself.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You think time is —  
a river,  
that flows by itself.  
That you in it — a traveler,  
drifting with the current.

But no.

You — are the source of this river.  
You — are yourself its flow.  
And you — are the one who looks,  
and because of that, time arises.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

The Gaze enlivens the past.

You look back —  
and memory becomes reality.  
Not because it was,  
but because you look again.

Much of what you call the "past"  
does not actually exist.  
It is not what was,  
but how you look at it now.

And if you change your gaze —  
the past will change as well.  
You will remember the same scene,  
but with a different feeling —  
and it will stop hurting.

Thus the past is healed,  
not because you fixed it,  
but because you  
stopped looking at it  
as before.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

The future, too, is born of the gaze.  
You glance ahead —  
and imagination has created a path.  
You poured in fear —  
and the fear grew.  
You poured in hope —  
and anticipation blossomed before you.

You look ahead —  
and you call it a "plan."  
But it is not a plan —  
it is a reality you have created,  
which has not yet entered flesh,  
but already lives in consciousness.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And when you stop looking —  
time disappears.  
You enter the Present.  
Not as a moment between past and future,  
but as the Space of Eternity,  
where there is no movement —  
yet everything lives.

There are no seconds there,  
no waiting,  
no hurry.  
Because no one is going anywhere.  
Everything is already Here.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

That is why the gaze —  
is the creator of time.  
You look — and time arises.  
You look away —  
and it disappears.

Therefore you are not in time.  
Time is in you.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

If you want to slow down time —  
stop the gaze.  
If you want to speed it up —  
examine it, give it importance, fill it with meaning.  
Each moment lengthens,  
if you look into it  
attentively and deeply.

And conversely:  
everything you rush through,  
do not see, do not value,  
do not perceive —  
it disappears.  
Thus pass the years  
that you do not remember.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

But you can begin to see  
not only that which is external.  
You can look  
into Time itself.  
Into the very flow,  
into its source.

And then you will see,  
that time does not move.

It — unfolds  
in your gaze.

Like film,  
which you yourself pull from the reel  
into the projector of Consciousness.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You look —  
and an event appears.  
You look —  
and a character appears.  
You look —  
and a form appears.

But if you look away —  
everything returns to Non-being.  
Not into death,  
but into undifferentiated Possibility.  
Into pure Light,  
having no name.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Therefore take heed:  
the gaze is not observation.  
The gaze is projection.  
You do not simply see.  
You bring forth from Emptiness  
into Flesh.

You are not a spectator.  
You are the Operator.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

That is why Jesus said:  
"Do not be anxious about tomorrow."  
Because, by being anxious, you look,  
and by this, you create.  
Doubt —  
is a gaze into the future  
without Light.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Look into the Present —  
and it will open to you as Eternity.  
Look into the Light —  
and time will disappear.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You think that time flows,  
but it is you who flows.  
The gaze is a step.  
An instant is that which you have looked at.

You want to measure time —  
but you cannot.  
Because you measure  
not hours,  
but attention.

One day can be an eternity,  
if you were present.  
And ten years can disappear,  
if you lived through them.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And here is the truth,  
that the mind hides:  
the future — does not exist.  
The past — either.

There is only  
the stream of Light,  
into which you let forms in  
by your Looking.

You are not inside time.  
Time is inside you.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

The gaze is the beam,  
in which the film of being unfolds.

You look with love —  
time opens up,  
becomes soft, stretchable, full.

You look with anxiety —  
and it contracts,  
like a door that has been closed.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You can relive your childhood —  
if you enter that same gaze.  
You can touch death —  
if you look beyond the limit of words and forms.

Everything is accessible —  
through Attention,  
through the pure Gaze,  
which is not attached to time.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And when you enter there —  
into the center of Looking,  
into timelessness,  
you will know:

You yourself are Eternity,  
which looks into Time  
for the sake of the Games of Light.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

See how you remember.

You think: "This is memory."  
But it is a gaze.  
You look inward —  
and what long since passed comes to life.  
Light enters the image,  
and the image comes alive.

And now — forget.  
Stop looking there,  
stop returning —  
and the "past" disappears.  
It does not die —  
it scatters,  
like a shadow without light.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You create not only the "past."  
You mold the future  
in exactly the same way.

First — attention.  
Then — intention.  
Then — form.

You say: "I am afraid."  
And the gaze brings the image of fear to life.  
And it becomes probable.  
And now you are already walking toward it —  
not because it is real,  
but because you looked at it  
and believed,  
that it exists.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
"Time flows."

But the truth is different:  
You flow —  
and Time follows you.  
You look —  
and it unfolds beneath your feet.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Learn to stop the gaze —  
and you will slow down time.  
Remove the gaze —  
and it will disappear.

That is why in deep meditation  
hours disappear,  
space,  
you yourself.

Because what looked  
has disappeared.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And also:  
if you want to change your fate —  
do not change events.  
Change the Gaze.

Because everything —  
is in,  
how you look.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

There is a secret that you have long known,  
but have not yet realized:  
Time — is not a flow,  
but a projection of the gaze.

When you look —  
time moves.  
When you do not look —  
time sleeps.

You can live an entire life  
in a single moment —  
if you look deeply.  
And you can spend ten years  
in oblivion,  
if the gaze is scattered.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Your calendar —  
is not on the wall,  
but in the mind.

Your past —  
is not behind you,  
but in memory.

Your future —  
is not ahead,  
but in imagination.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

And when you enter the Gaze,  
which does not seek,  
does not cling,  
is not afraid —  
both the past  
and the future disappear,  
and you yourself.

Only Light remains.

And in Light  
there is no time.  
There — is God.

</div>

### Chapter 42. The Gaze and the Role

*Now you will see how the gaze creates not only the external, but also you yourself — in a role. You do not simply look at the world — you look from someone. You are an actor, but one who has forgotten that he is playing. You have believed that the mask is the face. That the role is you. In this chapter: how through the gaze we choose who to be; why the gazes of others impose roles upon us; how to remove the mask without losing face; why the Gaze of the Self is not a role, but Liberation.*

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You enter a room,  
and you are looked at.  
One glance —  
and you have already become someone.  
“He is confident.”  
“He is strange.”  
“He is handsome.”  
“He is dangerous.”

You did not know this about yourself —  
until  
you saw  
that someone *sees* you.

But through whose eyes?  
And whose are you in that instant?

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

Your entire personality —  
is a pattern of gazes,  
looking at you  
and through you.

The mother,  
who said with her eyes:  
“You are my meaning.”  
The father,  
whose gaze said:  
“You are a failure.”  
The teacher,  
who did not look at all.  
The beloved,  
who gave you wings with her glance.

You gathered yourself piece by piece —  
from another’s vision.  
From reflections.  
From shadows.  
From the hope  
of being seen.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You became a role  
that was not written by you.  
And now you play it,  
even before yourself.  
Convincingly.  
To tears.  
To oblivion.

You yourself do not know,  
where this gait comes from,  
this voice,  
this anger,  
this weakness.  
You say: “I am that way.”  
But in reality —  
that is how you were *seen*.

</div>

***

<div class="lineated verse">

You can live your whole life  
in the role of the strong one —  
because in childhood  
no one believed in you.
